var
    $PLAYER1: Player
    $scplayer: Char

//-------------MAIN---------------
script_name 'MAIN'
Camera.DoFade(0, Fade.Out)
Game.SetMaxWantedLevel(2)
set_deatharrest_state 0
Clock.SetTimeOfDay(21, 0)
Streaming.RequestCollision(-535.64, -300.451)
Streaming.LoadScene(-535.64, -300.451, 12.29)
$PLAYER1 = Player.Create(0, 405.0, -905.0, 11.0712)
$scplayer = Player.GetChar($PLAYER1)
Weather.ForceNow(WeatherType.Foggy)
wait 0
declare_mission_flag $ONMISSION
if 
  not Char.IsDead($scplayer)
goto_if_false @MAIN_149
Char.Undress($scplayer, 'IGMERC')
Streaming.LoadAllModelsNow
Char.Dress($scplayer)
$ONMISSION = 0

:MAIN_149
wait 250
if 
    Player.IsPlaying($PLAYER1)
goto_if_false @MAIN_150
    Streaming.SetAreaVisible(Interior.MainMap)
    Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, False)
    Mission.LoadAndLaunchInternal(0)
    start_new_script @Star 
    start_new_script @Save
    start_new_script @VPHotel 
    start_new_script @Package
goto @MAIN_151

:MAIN_150
wait 500
if
  not Player.IsPlaying($PLAYER1)
goto @MAIN_149

:MAIN_151
wait 500
goto @MAIN_151

goto_if_false @Star_159
Sphere.Remove($SidewalkSphere)
Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, False)
Text.PrintBigString("Answering the Call to Abandon...", 3000, TextStyle.BottomRight)

Mission.LoadAndLaunchInternal(1)

:Fae_802
wait 0
if and
    Player.LocateAnyMeans3D($PLAYER1, 602.3546, -1700.3068, 6.2431, 5.0, 5.0, 5.0, False)
    Player.IsInModel($PLAYER1, #SPEEDER)
then
    if
        not $SpeederDelivered == 1
    then
        Text.PrintHelp('SPEED')
        wait 5000
        goto @Fae_1000
    else
        goto @Fae_911
    end

    goto @Fae_803

    $BarrierWater == 1
then
    if
        Char.IsInWater($scplayer)
    then
        Text.PrintHelpForever('TPORT2')
        goto @Water_20
    else
        goto @Water_50
    end

        $BarrierWater == 0
    then
        goto @Water_60
    end

wait 0

    Pad.IsKeyPressed(KeyCode.N)
then
    if
        Player.IsInAnyCar($PLAYER1)
    then
        Text.ClearHelp()

        wait 500
        Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, False)
        Player.WarpFromCarToCoord($PLAYER1, 315.7423, -1164.2609, 11.0712)
        wait 500
        Camera.DoFade(500, Fade.In)
        wait 500
        Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, True)
    else
        if
            not Player.IsInAnyCar($PLAYER1)
        then
            Text.ClearHelp()
            Camera.DoFade(500, Fade.Out)
            wait 500
            Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, False)
            Player.SetCoordinates($PLAYER1, 315.7423, -1164.2609, 11.0712)
            wait 500
            Camera.DoFade(500, Fade.In)
            wait 500
            Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, True)
            goto @Water_60
        end
    end
else
    if
        not Pad.IsKeyPressed(KeyCode.N)
    then
        goto @Water_70
    else
        goto @Water_20
    end
end

:Water_50
wait 500

    not Char.IsInWater($scplayer)
then
    goto @Water_60
else
    goto @Water_10
end

:Endgame
script_name 'Endgame'
wait 250
Streaming.RequestModel(#SABRE)
Streaming.RequestModel(#WFYG1)
wait 500
if or
  not Streaming.HasModelLoaded(#SABRE)
  not Streaming.HasModelLoaded(#WFYG1)
goto_if_false @Endgame_180
goto @Endgame_65

:Endgame_65
Streaming.LoadAllModelsNow
wait 500
if or
  Streaming.HasModelLoaded(#SABRE)
  Streaming.HasModelLoaded(#WFYG1)
goto_if_false @Endgame_65
goto @Endgame_180

:Endgame_99
$ONMISSION = 1
wait 500
Char.SetCoordinates($scplayer, -530.8, -320.328, 12.0)
Char.Delete($EndOfGamePed)
$ONMISSION = 0
Player.SetControl($scplayer, True)
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.Out)
wait 1500

:Endgame_180
Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, False)
$Sabre = Car.Create(#SABRE, -535.8, -323.328, 12.0)
wait 500
$EndOfGamePed = Char.Create(PedType.CivFemale, #WFYG1, -530.692, -315.928, 13.62)
wait 500
Camera.PointAtChar($EndOfGamePed, CameraMode.FollowPed, SwitchType.JumpCut)
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.In)
wait 1500
goto @Endgame_272

:Endgame_272
Char.SetObjEnterCarAsDriver($scplayer, $Sabre)
Char.SetObjEnterCarAsPassenger($EndOfGamePed, $Sabre)
wait 5000
if and
  Char.IsInCar($scplayer, $Sabre)
  Char.IsInCar($EndOfGamePed, $Sabre)
goto_if_false @Endgame_372
goto @Endgame_327

:Endgame_327
Camera.PointAtCar($Sabre, CameraMode.BehindCar, SwitchType.JumpCut)
Car.AddUpsidedownCheck($Sabre)
Car.GotoCoordinatesAccurate($Sabre, 240.4, -1280.2, 10.0)
Audio.PlayEndOfGameTune
goto @Endgame_438

:Endgame_372
wait 5000
if or
  Char.IsStuck($EndOfGamePed)
  Char.IsStuck($scplayer)
goto_if_false @Endgame_405
Char.SetCoordinates($EndOfGamePed, -530.692, -315.928, 13.62)
Char.SetCoordinates($scplayer, -530.8, -320.328, 12.0)
goto @Endgame_272

:Endgame_405
wait 5000
if or
  not Char.IsStuck($EndOfGamePed)
  not Char.IsStuck($scplayer)
goto_if_false @Endgame_99
goto @Endgame_327

:Endgame_438
wait 90000
if 
  Car.IsStoppedInArea2D($Sabre, 235.4, -1275.2, 245.6, -1285.6, 0)
goto_if_false @Endgame_511
if or
  not Car.IsInWater($Sabre)
  not Car.IsUpsidedown($Sabre)
goto_if_false @Endgame_618
goto @Endgame_662

:Endgame_511
wait 30000
if 
  not Car.IsStoppedInArea2D($Sabre, 235.4, -1275.2, 245.6, -1285.6, 0)
goto_if_false @Endgame_662
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.Out)
wait 1500
Camera.PointAtChar($EndOfGamePed, CameraMode.FollowPed, SwitchType.JumpCut)
Audio.StopEndOfGameTune
Char.SetObjLeaveCar($EndOfGamePed, $Sabre)
Char.SetObjLeaveCar($scplayer, $Sabre)
Stat.PlayerMadeProgress(20)
$Endgame = 1
$ONMISSION = 0
goto @Endgame_676

:Endgame_618
wait 0
if or
  Car.IsInWater($Sabre)
  Car.IsUpsidedown($Sabre)
goto_if_false @Endgame_511
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.Out)
wait 1500
goto @Endgame_99

:Endgame_662
Car.SetMission($Sabre, CarMission.GotoCoordsAsthecrowSwims)
goto @Endgame_511

:Endgame_676
wait 250
if 
  Player.IsPlaying($PLAYER1)
goto_if_false @Endgame_728
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.In)
wait 1500
Char.SetObjDestroyCar($EndOfGamePed, $Sabre)
Player.SetControl($PLAYER1, True)
terminate_this_script 
return 

:Endgame_728
wait 250
if 
  not Player.IsPlaying($PLAYER1)
goto_if_false @Endgame_676
wait 5000
Camera.PointAtChar($EndOfGamePed, CameraMode.FollowPed, SwitchType.JumpCut)
Car.LockDoors($Sabre, CarLock.LockedPlayerInside)
Char.SetObjDestroyCar($EndOfGamePed, $Sabre)
Camera.DoFade(1500, Fade.In)
wait 1500

:Endgame_729
wait 500
if
    Player.IsPlaying($PLAYER1)
then
    Text.Print('Endgame', 5000, 0) // Go watch the mindless destruction!
    Camera.SetInFrontOfPlayer()
    goto @Endgame_730
else
    wait 500
    goto @Endgame_728
end

:Endgame_730
terminate_this_script
